Real Estate Investment Trusts (REITs) are companies that own or finance real estate properties and provide a way for individuals to invest in real estate without directly owning physical properties. In India, REITs are regulated by the Securities and Exchange Board of India (SEBI) and are listed on the stock exchanges.
